creations-chat 2021-02-24 14:29:30 That Tie Infiltrator is not worthy of a hundred upvotes neither will it ever be in HOF. There's really no reason to brag about upvotes when the true quality of the build really isn't *perfect*. Now moving on to actual criticism:
1. The paint should be less scattered and put into the actual places. Using trails could help, though I understand if you can't achieve that as it's a pretty hard thing to do.
2. The top and bottom parts of the main part of it should be rounded and not flat. The window is already as complex as it is so I wont really nitpick that. 
3. The arms that extend onto the wings could use a little detailing. For the most part they're fine but you could definitely fit some level of detail into them.

It overall looks like a nice Tie-Interceptor that doesn't have that much problems, you have the wings rotating which I haven't seen happen is a cool touchup.
This isn't to instigate drama, it's just feedback that you should take. The first part may be a bit aggressive but take this with a grain of salt. Have a good day mate.
